# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

## Summary

I've identified and documented the C++ source files in envoyproxy/envoy that implement both xDS v2 and v3 API handling for the ADS gRPC server. The key findings include:

**Core Implementation Components:**

1. **Unified xDS Mux** (`source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/`): Template-based `GrpcMuxImpl<S, F, RQ, RS>` class supporting both SotW and Delta protocols with configurable v2/v3 proto types

2. **Subscription Management**: `SotwSubscriptionState` and `DeltaSubscriptionState` classes manage protocol state with v2/v3 compatibility

3. **Subscription Factory**: `GrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory`, `DeltaGrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory`, and `AdsConfigSubscriptionFactory` create subscriptions based on API version configuration

4. **Resource Handling**: `decoded_resource_impl.h` and `opaque_resource_decoder_impl.h` provide versioned resource decoding

5. **Proto Migration Annotations**: v2 proto files include `(udpa.annotations.field_migrate)` annotations for field name transitions to v3

6. **Runtime Version Control**: The `transport_api_version` and `resource_api_version` fields in `ApiConfigSource` control which API version is used

The answer includes 20 relevant files, 9 key symbols, a call chain demonstrating the subscription creation flow, and comprehensive narrative documentation explaining the architecture.

            "content": "7: \n8: # API semantic versioning\n9: \n10: The Envoy APIs consist of a family of packages, e.g. `envoy.admin.v3alpha`,\n11: `envoy.service.trace.v3`. Each package is independently versioned with a protobuf semantic\n12: versioning scheme based on https://cloud.google.com/apis/design/versioning.\n13: \n14: The major version for a package is captured in its name (and directory structure). E.g. version 3\n15: of the tracing API package is named `envoy.service.trace.v3` and its constituent protos are located\n16: in `api/envoy/service/trace/v3`. Every protobuf must live directly in a versioned package namespace,\n17: we do not allow subpackages such as `envoy.service.trace.v3.somethingelse`.\n18: ",

`grpc_mux_impl.cc`: Contains the template-based `GrpcMuxImpl<S, F, RQ, RS>` class that handles both SotW (State of the World) and Delta discovery protocols. The template parameters RQ and RS represent the request and response proto types, supporting both v2 (DiscoveryRequest/DiscoveryResponse) and v3 (DiscoveryRequest v3/DiscoveryResponse v3) types.\\n   - `sotw_subscription_state.h` and `sotw_subscription_state.cc`: Manages subscription state for SotW protocol with v2/v3 compatibility.\\n   - `delta_subscription_state.h` and `delta_subscription_state.cc`: Manages subscription state for Delta protocol with v2/v3 compatibility.\\n   - `subscription_state.h`: Base interface for subscription state management.\\n\\n2. **Legacy GrpcMux Implementation (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/):**\\n   - `grpc_mux_impl.h` and `grpc_mux_impl.cc`: Legacy SotW-only GrpcMux implementation using v3 discovery types (envoy::service::discovery::v3::DiscoveryRequest/Response).\\n   - `new_grpc_mux_impl.h` and `new_grpc_mux_impl.cc`: New Delta-only GrpcMux implementation using v3 discovery types (envoy::service::discovery::v3::DeltaDiscoveryRequest/Response).\\n\\n3. **Subscription Factory (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/):**\\n   - `grpc_subscription_factory.h` and `grpc_subscription_factory.cc`: Creates subscriptions for SotW GRPC, Delta GRPC, and ADS. The factory handles API version configuration through the `transport_api_version` field in `ApiConfigSource`.\\n\\n4. **Failover Support:**\\n   - `grpc_mux_failover.h`: Implements failover logic between primary and secondary xDS sources with v2/v3 proto type support through template parameters.\\n\\n5. **Resource Decoding and Management:**\\n   - `source/common/config/decoded_resource_impl.h`: Handles decoded resource representation with support for versioned proto types.\\n   - `source/common/config/opaque_resource_decoder_impl.h`: Resource decoder that maintains v2/v3 compatibility.\\n   - `source/common/config/xds_manager_impl.h` and `xds_manager_impl.cc`: Manages multiple xDS subscriptions with v2/v3 version awareness.\\n   - `source/common/config/subscription_factory_impl.h` and `subscription_factory_impl.cc`: Creates subscriptions based on ConfigSource configuration.\\n\\n6. **Proto Link Hacks:**\\n   - `source/common/config/protobuf_link_hacks.h`: Forces linking of v3 proto definitions.\\n   - `test/config/v2_link_hacks.h`: Forces linking of v2 proto definitions for testing.\\n\\n**Key Field Renames and Migration Patterns:**\\n\\nThe v2-to-v3 migration is defined in the proto files with `(udpa.annotations.field_migrate)` annotations:\\n- `api/envoy/api/v2/discovery.proto`: Defines v2 DiscoveryRequest and DeltaDiscoveryRequest messages that are annotated to migrate to v3.\\n- `api/envoy/api/v2/core/config_source.proto`: Defines ApiVersion enum with V2 (deprecated) and V3 values, controlling transport API version selection.\\n\\n**ADS gRPC Server and Dual-Version Handling:**\\n\\nThe ADS implementation supports both v2 and v3 through:\\n1. **Runtime Feature Flags**: The unified mux uses `envoy.reloadable_features.unified_mux` to select between legacy (GrpcMuxImpl, NewGrpcMuxImpl) and unified implementations (Config::XdsMux::GrpcMuxSotw, Config::XdsMux::GrpcMuxDelta).\\n2. **Template-Based Protocol Handling**: The xds_mux `GrpcMuxImpl<S, F, RQ, RS>` template allows single codebase to handle both SotW and Delta with v2 or v3 proto types.\\n3. **API Version Configuration**: The `transport_api_version` field in `ApiConfigSource` controls which protocol version is used on the wire, while `resource_api_version` controls the resource message versions.\\n\\n**Subscription Lifecycle:**\\n\\nWhen a subscription is created (in `GrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory::create`), the factory determines the appropriate Mux implementation based on:\\n1. The API type (GRPC for SotW, DELTA_GRPC for Delta)\\n2. Whether the unified mux feature is enabled\\n3. The transport_api_version setting (though v2 is now deprecated)\\n\\nThe subscription then uses the selected mux to send discovery requests and handle responses through the appropriate SubscriptionState implementation (SotwSubscriptionState or DeltaSubscriptionState).\"\n}\nEOF\ncat /workspace/answer.json\n"

infrastructure.\\n\\n**Primary Implementation Files:**\\n\\n1. **Unified xDS Mux Implementation (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/):**\\n   - `grpc_mux_impl.h` and `grpc_mux_impl.cc`: Contains the template-based `GrpcMuxImpl<S, F, RQ, RS>` class that handles both SotW (State of the World) and Delta discovery protocols. The template parameters RQ and RS represent the request and response proto types, supporting both v2 (DiscoveryRequest/DiscoveryResponse) and v3 (DiscoveryRequest v3/DiscoveryResponse v3) types.\\n   - `sotw_subscription_state.h` and `sotw_subscription_state.cc`: Manages subscription state for SotW protocol with v2/v3 compatibility.\\n   - `delta_subscription_state.h` and `delta_subscription_state.cc`: Manages subscription state for Delta protocol with v2/v3 compatibility.\\n   - `subscription_state.h`: Base interface for subscription state management.\\n\\n2. **Legacy GrpcMux Implementation (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/):**\\n   - `grpc_mux_impl.h` and `grpc_mux_impl.cc`: Legacy SotW-only GrpcMux implementation using v3 discovery types (envoy::service::discovery::v3::DiscoveryRequest/Response).\\n   - `new_grpc_mux_impl.h` and `new_grpc_mux_impl.cc`: New Delta-only GrpcMux implementation using v3 discovery types (envoy::service::discovery::v3::DeltaDiscoveryRequest/Response).\\n\\n3. **Subscription Factory (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/):**\\n   - `grpc_subscription_factory.h` and `grpc_subscription_factory.cc`: Creates subscriptions for SotW GRPC, Delta GRPC, and ADS. The factory handles API version configuration through the `transport_api_version` field in `ApiConfigSource`.\\n\\n4. **Failover Support:**\\n   - `grpc_mux_failover.h`: Implements failover logic between primary and secondary xDS sources with v2/v3 proto type support through template parameters.\\n\\n5. **Resource Decoding and Management:**\\n   - `source/common/config/decoded_resource_impl.h`: Handles decoded resource representation with support for versioned proto types.\\n   - `source/common/config/opaque_resource_decoder_impl.h`: Resource decoder that maintains v2/v3 compatibility.\\n   - `source/common/config/xds_manager_impl.h` and `xds_manager_impl.cc`: Manages multiple xDS subscriptions with v2/v3 version awareness.\\n   - `source/common/config/subscription_factory_impl.h` and `subscription_factory_impl.cc`: Creates subscriptions based on ConfigSource configuration.\\n\\n6. **Proto Link Hacks:**\\n   - `source/common/config/protobuf_link_hacks.h`: Forces linking of v3 proto definitions.\\n   - `test/config/v2_link_hacks.h`: Forces linking of v2 proto definitions for testing.\\n\\n**Key Field Renames and Migration Patterns:**\\n\\nThe v2-to-v3 migration is defined in the proto files with `(udpa.annotations.field_migrate)` annotations:\\n- `api/envoy/api/v2/discovery.proto`: Defines v2 DiscoveryRequest and DeltaDiscoveryRequest messages that are annotated to migrate to v3.\\n- `api/envoy/api/v2/core/config_source.proto`: Defines ApiVersion enum with V2 (deprecated) and V3 values, controlling transport API version selection.\\n\\n**ADS gRPC Server and Dual-Version Handling:**\\n\\nThe ADS implementation supports both v2 and v3 through:\\n1. **Runtime Feature Flags**: The unified mux uses `envoy.reloadable_features.unified_mux` to select between legacy (GrpcMuxImpl, NewGrpcMuxImpl) and unified implementations (Config::XdsMux::GrpcMuxSotw, Config::XdsMux::GrpcMuxDelta).\\n2. **Template-Based Protocol Handling**: The xds_mux `GrpcMuxImpl<S, F, RQ, RS>` template allows single codebase to handle both SotW and Delta with v2 or v3 proto types.\\n3. **API Version Configuration**: The `transport_api_version` field in `ApiConfigSource` controls which protocol version is used on the wire, while `resource_api_version` controls the resource message versions.\\n\\n**Subscription Lifecycle:**\\n\\nWhen a subscription is created (in `GrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory::create`), the factory determines the appropriate Mux implementation based on:\\n1. The API type (GRPC for SotW, DELTA_GRPC for Delta)\\n2. Whether the unified mux feature is enabled\\n3. The transport_api_version setting (though v2 is now deprecated)\\n\\nThe subscription then uses the selected mux to send discovery requests and handle responses through the appropriate SubscriptionState implementation (SotwSubscriptionState or DeltaSubscriptionState).\"\n}"
}
